CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Users](
	[UserID] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
	[UserName] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[Password] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[Email] [nvarchar](100) NOT NULL,
	[LastPasswordChange] [datetime] NULL,
	[LastLoginDate] [datetime] NULL,
	[DateCreate] [datetime] NULL,
	[User_ToString] [nvarchar](100) NULL,
	[Type] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[Active] [bit] NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [PK_User] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[UserID] ASC
) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[NhapDiem_Update]	@IDNhapDiem           int,	@MonHoc               int,	@GiaoVien             int,	@NgayNhap             datetime,	@DotThi               int,	@NgayHetHanNhap       datetime,	@FileDPF              nvarchar(500),	@FileExcel            nvarchar(500),	@Hit int,	@Modify int,	@Download intASUPDATE NhapDiem SET 	MonHoc= @MonHoc,	GiaoVien= @GiaoVien,	NgayNhap= @NgayNhap,	DotThi= @DotThi,	NgayHetHanNhap= @NgayHetHanNhap,	FileDPF= @FileDPF,	FileExcel= @FileExcel,	Hit = @Hit,	Modify = @Modify,	Download = @DownloadWHERE IDNhapDiem = @IDNhapDiem
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[NhapDiem_Single]	@IDNhapDiem  intAS	SET NOCOUNT ON	SELECT * FROM NhapDiem  WHERE IDNhapDiem = @IDNhapDiem
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[NhapDiem_PagingIDDotThi]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create PROCEDURE [dbo].[NhapDiem_PagingIDDotThi]	@PageNumber  int,	@PageSize  int,	@IDDotthi intASDECLARE @_NhapDiem TABLE (	RowNumber INT IDENTITY (1,1), 	IDNhapDiem           int, 	MonHoc               int, 	GiaoVien             int, 	NgayNhap             datetime, 	DotThi               int, 	NgayHetHanNhap       datetime, 	FileDPF              nvarchar(500), 	FileExcel            nvarchar(500),	Hit	int,	Modify int,	Download int)INSERT INTO @_NhapDiemSELECT IDNhapDiem, MonHoc, GiaoVien, NgayNhap, DotThi, NgayHetHanNhap, FileDPF, FileExcel, Hit, Modify, DownloadFROM NhapDiem where @IDDotThi=DotThi order by IDNhapDiem descSELECT COUNT (IDNhapDiem) FROM @_NhapDiemSELECT * FROM @_NhapDiem WHERE RowNumber > (@PageNumber -1) * @PageSize AND RowNumber <=@PageNumber * @PageSize
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[NhapDiem_Paging]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[NhapDiem_Paging]	@PageNumber  int,	@PageSize  intASDECLARE @_NhapDiem TABLE (	RowNumber INT IDENTITY (1,1), 	IDNhapDiem           int, 	MonHoc               int, 	GiaoVien             int, 	NgayNhap             datetime, 	DotThi               int, 	NgayHetHanNhap       datetime, 	FileDPF              nvarchar(500), 	FileExcel            nvarchar(500),	Hit	int,	Modify int,	Download int)INSERT INTO @_NhapDiemSELECT IDNhapDiem, MonHoc, GiaoVien, NgayNhap, DotThi, NgayHetHanNhap, FileDPF, FileExcel, Hit, Modify, DownloadFROM NhapDiemSELECT COUNT (IDNhapDiem) FROM @_NhapDiemSELECT * FROM @_NhapDiem WHERE RowNumber > (@PageNumber -1) * @PageSize AND RowNumber <=@PageNumber * @PageSize
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[NhapDiem_AddMissGIAOVIEN]	@IDNhapDiem           int  output,	@MonHoc               int,	@NgayNhap             datetime,	@DotThi               int,	@NgayHetHanNhap       datetime,	@FileDPF              nvarchar(500),	@FileExcel            nvarchar(500),	@Hit					int,@Modify	int,@Download intASINSERT INTO NhapDiem(	MonHoc,	NgayNhap,	DotThi,	NgayHetHanNhap,	FileDPF,		FileExcel,Hit,Modify,Download)VALUES (	@MonHoc,	@NgayNhap,	@DotThi,	@NgayHetHanNhap,	@FileDPF,	@FileExcel,@Hit,@Modify,@Download)SET @IDNhapDiem = @@IDENTITY
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure MonHoc_Update    Generate Code Date: 6/8/2011 2:42:37 PM ******/CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[MonHoc_Update]	@IDMonHoc             int,	@MaMH                 nvarchar(10),	@TenMH                nvarchar(500),	@SoTC                 int,	@Khoa                 int,	@Active               bitASUPDATE MonHoc SET 	MaMH= @MaMH,	TenMH= @TenMH,	SoTC= @SoTC,	Khoa= @Khoa,	Active= @ActiveWHERE IDMonHoc = @IDMonHoc
GO

create PROCEDURE [dbo].[MonHoc_Paging2]	@PageNumber  int,	@PageSize  intASDECLARE @_MonHoc TABLE (	RowNumber INT, 	IDMonHoc             int, 	MaMH                 nvarchar(10), 	TenMH                nvarchar(500), 	SoTC                 int, 	Khoa                 int, 	Active               bit)INSERT INTO @_MonHocSELECT ROW_NUMBER() over (ORDER BY IDMONHOC) as Row, IDMonHoc, MaMH, TenMH, SoTC, Khoa, ActiveFROM MonHocSELECT COUNT (IDMonHoc) FROM @_MonHocSELECT * FROM @_MonHoc WHERE RowNumber > (@PageNumber -1) * @PageSize						 AND RowNumber <=@PageNumber * @PageSize
GO

GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Khoa_Paging]	@PageNumber  int,	@PageSize  intASDECLARE @_Khoa TABLE (	RowNumber INT IDENTITY (1,1), 	IDKhoa               int, 	TenKhoa              nvarchar(1000), 	Active               bit)INSERT INTO @_KhoaSELECT IDKhoa, TenKhoa, ActiveFROM KhoaSELECT COUNT (IDKhoa) FROM @_KhoaSELECT * FROM @_Khoa WHERE RowNumber > (@PageNumber -1) * @PageSize AND RowNumber <=@PageNumber * @PageSize
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure DotThi_Update    Generate Code Date: 7/6/2011 2:53:16 PM ******/create PROCEDURE [dbo].[DotThi_Update]	@IDDotThi             int,	@TenDotThi            nvarchar(1000),	@HocKy                int,	@NamHoc               nvarchar(20),	@Khoa                 int,	@Active               bitASUPDATE DotThi SET 	TenDotThi= @TenDotThi,	HocKy= @HocKy,	NamHoc= @NamHoc,	Khoa= @Khoa,	Active= @ActiveWHERE IDDotThi = @IDDotThi
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[DotThi_Single]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[DotThi_Single]	@IDDotThi  intAS	SET NOCOUNT ON	SELECT * FROM DotThi  WHERE IDDotThi = @IDDotThi
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[DotThi_Paging]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[DotThi_Paging]	@PageNumber  int,	@PageSize  intASDECLARE @_DotThi TABLE (	RowNumber INT IDENTITY (1,1), 	IDDotThi             int, 	TenDotThi            nvarchar(1000), 	HocKy                int, 	NamHoc               nvarchar(20), 	Khoa                 int, 	Active               bit)INSERT INTO @_DotThiSELECT IDDotThi, TenDotThi, HocKy, NamHoc, Khoa, ActiveFROM DotThiSELECT COUNT (IDDotThi) FROM @_DotThiSELECT * FROM @_DotThi WHERE RowNumber > (@PageNumber -1) * @PageSize AND RowNumber <=@PageNumber * @PageSize
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[DotThi_FindByAll]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
Create PROCEDURE [dbo].[DotThi_FindByAll]@TenDotThi nvarchar(1000),@HocKy int,@NamHoc nvarchar(30),@Khoa intASSELECT * FROM [DotThi] where @TenDotThi = TenDotThi and @HocKy= HocKy and @NamHoc = NamHoc and @Khoa=Khoa
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[DotThi_Add]	@IDDotThi             int  output,	@TenDotThi            nvarchar(1000),	@HocKy                int,	@NamHoc               nvarchar(20),	@Khoa                 int,	@Active               bitASINSERT INTO DotThi(	TenDotThi,	HocKy,	NamHoc,	Khoa,	Active)VALUES (	@TenDotThi,	@HocKy,	@NamHoc,	@Khoa,	@Active)SET @IDDotThi = @@IDENTITY
GO

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Application](
	[ApplicationID] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
	[Application_Name] [nvarchar](500) NOT NULL,
	[Application_Description] [ntext] NULL,
	[Application_FilePath] [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	[Application_Image] [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	[Application_DateCreate] [datetime] NULL,
	[Application_ToString] [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	[Parent_Id] [int] NULL,
	[Order] [int] NULL,
	[Active] [bit] NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [PK_Application] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[ApplicationID] ASC
) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY] TEXTIMAGE_ON [PRIMARY]

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Application_CreateDeleteUpdate]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
------------------------------------------------------------------
------------------ Procedure Table Application ---------------------------
------------------------------------------------------------------

 CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Application_CreateDeleteUpdate]
(
	@ApplicationID int out, 
	@Application_Name nvarchar(500),
	@Application_Description ntext,
	@Application_FilePath nvarchar(200),
	@Application_Image nvarchar(200),
	@Application_DateCreate datetime,
	@Application_ToString nvarchar(500),
	@Parent_Id int,
	@Active bit,
	@Action int)
AS
--Create
IF @Action = 0
 BEGIN
 INSERT INTO Application
	( [Application_Name], [Application_Description], [Application_FilePath], [Application_Image], [Application_DateCreate], [Application_ToString], [Parent_Id], [Active] )
 VALUES 
	( @Application_Name, @Application_Description, @Application_FilePath, @Application_Image, @Application_DateCreate, @Application_ToString, @Parent_Id, @Active)
 SET @ApplicationID = @@IDENTITY
END
--Delete 
ELSE IF @Action = 1
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT [ApplicationID] FROM Application WHERE [ApplicationID] = @ApplicationID)
		BEGIN
		UPDATE Application SET [Active] = 0 WHERE [ApplicationID] = @ApplicationID
		END	
END
--Update 
ELSE IF @Action = 2 
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT [ApplicationID] FROM Application WHERE [ApplicationID] = @ApplicationID)
		BEGIN
		UPDATE Application
		SET 
		[Application_Name] = @Application_Name,
		[Application_Description] = @Application_Description,
		[Application_FilePath] = @Application_FilePath,
		[Application_Image] = @Application_Image,
		[Application_DateCreate] = @Application_DateCreate,
		[Application_ToString] = @Application_ToString,
		[Parent_Id] = @Parent_Id,
		[Active] = @Active
 		WHERE [ApplicationID] = @ApplicationID
  		END
END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Application_Update]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure Application_Update    Generate Code Date: 6/17/2011 10:00:52 PM ******/CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Application_Update]	@ApplicationID        int,	@Application_Name     nvarchar(500),	@Application_Description ntext,	@Application_FilePath nvarchar(200),	@Application_Image    nvarchar(200),	@Application_DateCreate datetime,	@Application_ToString nvarchar(500),	@Parent_Id            int,	@Order                int,	@Active               bitASUPDATE Application SET 	Application_Name= @Application_Name,	Application_Description= @Application_Description,	Application_FilePath= @Application_FilePath,	Application_Image= @Application_Image,	Application_DateCreate= @Application_DateCreate,	Application_ToString= @Application_ToString,	Parent_Id= @Parent_Id,	[Order]= @Order,	Active= @ActiveWHERE ApplicationID = @ApplicationID
GO

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Application_Search]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create Procedure [dbo].[Application_Search]
(
	@ApplicationID int out, 
	@Application_Name nvarchar(500),	
	@Parent_Id int,	
	@Action int)
AS
--Search by Id
IF @Action = 0
	BEGIN
		SELECT * FROM Application WHERE ApplicationID=@ApplicationID
	END
--Search by Name 
ELSE IF @Action = 1
BEGIN
	SELECT * FROM Application where Application_Name like '%'+@Application_Name+'%' 		  		
END
--Search by Parent_Id 
ELSE IF @Action = 2 
BEGIN
	SELECT * FROM Application where Parent_Id=@Parent_Id
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Application_PagingByParent]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Application_PagingByParent]	@PageNumber  int,	@PageSize  int,	@parentID intASDECLARE @_Application TABLE (	RowNumber INT IDENTITY (1,1), 	ApplicationID        int, 	Application_Name     nvarchar(500), 	Application_Description ntext, 	Application_FilePath nvarchar(200), 	Application_Image    nvarchar(200), 	Application_DateCreate datetime, 	Application_ToString nvarchar(500), 	Parent_Id            int, 	[Order]                int, 	Active               bit)INSERT INTO @_ApplicationSELECT ApplicationID, Application_Name, Application_Description, Application_FilePath, Application_Image, Application_DateCreate, Application_ToString, Parent_Id, [Order], ActiveFROM [Application] where @parentID=Parent_Id order by ApplicationID descSELECT COUNT (ApplicationID) FROM @_ApplicationSELECT * FROM @_Application WHERE RowNumber > (@PageNumber -1) * @PageSize AND RowNumber <=@PageNumber * @PageSize
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Application_Paging]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create PROCEDURE [dbo].[Application_Paging]	@PageNumber  int,	@PageSize  intASDECLARE @_Application TABLE (	RowNumber INT IDENTITY (1,1), 	ApplicationID        int, 	Application_Name     nvarchar(500), 	Application_Description ntext, 	Application_FilePath nvarchar(200), 	Application_Image    nvarchar(200), 	Application_DateCreate datetime, 	Application_ToString nvarchar(500), 	Parent_Id            int, 	[Order]                int, 	Active               bit)INSERT INTO @_ApplicationSELECT ApplicationID, Application_Name, Application_Description, Application_FilePath, Application_Image, Application_DateCreate, Application_ToString, Parent_Id, [Order], ActiveFROM ApplicationSELECT COUNT (ApplicationID) FROM @_ApplicationSELECT * FROM @_Application WHERE RowNumber > (@PageNumber -1) * @PageSize AND RowNumber <=@PageNumber * @PageSize
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Group_CreateDeleteUpdate]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Group_CreateDeleteUpdate]
(
	@GroupID int out, 
	@Group_Name nvarchar(50),
	@Group_Description ntext,
	@Group_ToString nvarchar(50),
	@Group_DateCreate datetime,
	@User_Create int,
	@Active bit,
	@Action int)
AS
--Create
IF @Action = 0
 BEGIN
 INSERT INTO Groups
	( [Group_Name], [Group_Description], [Group_ToString], [Group_DateCreate], [User_Create], [Active] )
 VALUES 
	( @Group_Name, @Group_Description, @Group_ToString, @Group_DateCreate, @User_Create, @Active)
 SET @GroupID = @@IDENTITY
END
--Delete 
ELSE IF @Action = 1
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT [GroupID] FROM Groups WHERE [GroupID] = @GroupID)
		BEGIN
		UPDATE Groups
		SET 		
		[Active] = 0
 		WHERE [GroupID] = @GroupID
  		END
END
--Update 
ELSE IF @Action = 2 
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT [GroupID] FROM Groups WHERE [GroupID] = @GroupID)
		BEGIN
		UPDATE Groups
		SET 
		[Group_Name] = @Group_Name,
		[Group_Description] = @Group_Description,
		[Group_ToString] = @Group_ToString,
		[Group_DateCreate] = @Group_DateCreate,
		[User_Create] = @User_Create,
		[Active] = @Active
 		WHERE [GroupID] = @GroupID
  		END
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GiaoVien_Update]	@IDGiaoVien           int,	@HoGV                 nvarchar(500),	@TenGV                nvarchar(200),	@Email                nvarchar(200),	@DienThoai            nvarchar(15),	@Khoa                 int,	@Active               bitASUPDATE GiaoVien SET 	HoGV= @HoGV,	TenGV= @TenGV,	Email= @Email,	DienThoai= @DienThoai,	Khoa= @Khoa,	Active= @ActiveWHERE IDGiaoVien = @IDGiaoVien
GO

GO

GO
create Procedure [dbo].[Group_Search]
(
	@GroupID int out, 
	@Group_Name nvarchar(50),
	@Group_DateCreate datetime,	
	@User_Create int,	
	@Action int)
AS
--Search by GroupId
IF @Action = 0
 BEGIN
	 SELECT * FROM Groups WHERE GroupID=@GroupID
END
--Search by Group_Name
ELSE IF @Action = 1
BEGIN
	SELECT * FROM Groups WHERE Group_Name like '%'+@Group_Name+'%'
END
--Search by Datetime create 
ELSE IF @Action = 2 
BEGIN
	SELECT * FROM Groups WHERE Group_DateCreate=@Group_DateCreate
END
-- searhc by User_Create
ELSE IF @Action = 3 
BEGIN
	SELECT * FROM Groups WHERE User_Create=@User_Create
END
GO

create PROCEDURE [dbo].[Application_GetByParentID_IdGroup]
(	
	@ParentID int,
	@GroupID int
)
AS
select * from (select * from InRole where GroupID=@GroupID) g,Application ap where g.ApplicationID = ap.ApplicationID and Parent_Id=@ParentID

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure Permission_Update    Generate Code Date: 6/17/2011 10:04:10 PM ******/CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Permission_Update]	@PermissionID         int,	@Name                 nvarchar(100),	@Descritption         nvarchar(100),	@Permission_ToString  nvarchar(100),	@Active               bitASUPDATE Permission SET 	Name= @Name,	Descritption= @Descritption,	Permission_ToString= @Permission_ToString,	Active= @ActiveWHERE PermissionID = @PermissionID
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure Permission_Single    Generate Code Date: 6/17/2011 10:04:10 PM ******/CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Permission_Single]	@PermissionID  intAS	SET NOCOUNT ON	SELECT * FROM Permission  WHERE PermissionID = @PermissionID
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Permission_Search]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create Procedure [dbo].[Permission_Search]
(
	@PermissionID int out,
	@Name nvarchar(100), 		
	@Action int)
AS
--Search by PermissionID
IF @Action = 0
 BEGIN
	 SELECT * FROM Permission WHERE PermissionID=@PermissionID
END
--Search by Name
ELSE IF @Action = 1
BEGIN
	SELECT * FROM Permission WHERE Name like '%'+@Name+'%'
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Permission_Paging]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure Permission_Paging    Generate Code Date: 6/17/2011 10:04:10 PM ******/CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Permission_Paging]	@PageNumber  int,	@PageSize  intASDECLARE @_Permission TABLE (	RowNumber INT IDENTITY (1,1), 	PermissionID         int, 	Name                 nvarchar(100), 	Descritption         nvarchar(100), 	Permission_ToString  nvarchar(100), 	Active               bit)INSERT INTO @_PermissionSELECT PermissionID, Name, Descritption, Permission_ToString, ActiveFROM PermissionSELECT COUNT (PermissionID) FROM @_PermissionSELECT * FROM @_Permission WHERE RowNumber > (@PageNumber -1) * @PageSize AND RowNumber <=@PageNumber * @PageSize
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON

------------------------------------------------------------------
------------------ Procedure Table Permission ---------------------------
------------------------------------------------------------------

 CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Permission_CreateDeleteUpdate]
(
	@PermissionID int out, 
	@Name nvarchar(100),
	@Descritption nvarchar(100),
	@Permission_ToString nvarchar(100),
	@Active bit,
	@Action int)
AS
--Create
IF @Action = 0
 BEGIN
 INSERT INTO Permission
	( [Name], [Descritption], [Permission_ToString], [Active] )
 VALUES 
	( @Name, @Descritption, @Permission_ToString, @Active)
 SET @PermissionID = @@IDENTITY
END
--Delete 
ELSE IF @Action = 1
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT [PermissionID] FROM Permission WHERE [PermissionID] = @PermissionID)
		BEGIN
		UPDATE Permission
		SET 		
		[Active] = 0
 		WHERE [PermissionID] = @PermissionID
  		END
END
--Update 
ELSE IF @Action = 2 
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT [PermissionID] FROM Permission WHERE [PermissionID] = @PermissionID)
		BEGIN
		UPDATE Permission
		SET 
		[Name] = @Name,
		[Descritption] = @Descritption,
		[Permission_ToString] = @Permission_ToString,
		[Active] = @Active
 		WHERE [PermissionID] = @PermissionID
  		END
END
GO

GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure Setting_Paging    Generate Code Date: 6/17/2011 10:04:10 PM ******/CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Setting_Paging]	@PageNumber  int,	@PageSize  intASDECLARE @_Setting TABLE (	RowNumber INT IDENTITY (1,1), 	SettingID            int, 	Setting_Name         nvarchar(100), 	Setting_Description  ntext, 	Setting_DateCreate   datetime, 	Value                nvarchar(50), 	Active               bit)INSERT INTO @_SettingSELECT SettingID, Setting_Name, Setting_Description, Setting_DateCreate, Value, ActiveFROM SettingSELECT COUNT (SettingID) FROM @_SettingSELECT * FROM @_Setting WHERE RowNumber > (@PageNumber -1) * @PageSize AND RowNumber <=@PageNumber * @PageSize

 CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Setting_CreateDeleteUpdate]
(
	@SettingID int out, 
	@Setting_Name nvarchar(100),
	@Setting_Description ntext,
	@Setting_DateCreate datetime,
	@Value nvarchar(50),
	@Active bit,
	@Action int)
AS
--Create
IF @Action = 0
 BEGIN
 INSERT INTO Setting
	( [Setting_Name], [Setting_Description], [Setting_DateCreate], [Value], [Active] )
 VALUES 
	( @Setting_Name, @Setting_Description, @Setting_DateCreate, @Value, @Active)
 SET @SettingID = @@IDENTITY
END
--Delete 
ELSE IF @Action = 1
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT [SettingID] FROM Setting WHERE [SettingID] = @SettingID)
		BEGIN
		UPDATE Setting
		SET 		
		[Active] = 0
 		WHERE [SettingID] = @SettingID
  		END
END
--Update 
ELSE IF @Action = 2 
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT [SettingID] FROM Setting WHERE [SettingID] = @SettingID)
		BEGIN
		UPDATE Setting
		SET 
		[Setting_Name] = @Setting_Name,
		[Setting_Description] = @Setting_Description,
		[Setting_DateCreate] = @Setting_DateCreate,
		[Value] = @Value,
		[Active] = @Active
 		WHERE [SettingID] = @SettingID
  		END
END

	[LogID] ASC
) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Users_CreateDeleteUpdate]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
------------------------------------------------------------------
------------------ Procedure Table Users ---------------------------
------------------------------------------------------------------

 CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Users_CreateDeleteUpdate]
(
	@UserID int out, 
	@UserName nvarchar(50),
	@Password nvarchar(50),
	@Email nvarchar(100),
	@LastPasswordChange datetime,
	@LastLoginDate datetime,
	@DateCreate datetime,
	@User_ToString nvarchar(100),
	@Type nvarchar(50),
	@Active bit,
	@Action int)
AS
--Create
IF @Action = 0
 BEGIN
 INSERT INTO Users
	( [UserName], [Password], [Email], [LastPasswordChange], [LastLoginDate], [DateCreate], [User_ToString], [Type], [Active] )
 VALUES 
	( @UserName, @Password, @Email, @LastPasswordChange, @LastLoginDate, @DateCreate, @User_ToString, @Type, @Active)
 SET @UserID = @@IDENTITY
END
--Delete 
ELSE IF @Action = 1
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT [UserID] FROM Users WHERE [UserID] = @UserID)
		BEGIN
		UPDATE Users
		SET 		
		[Active] = 0
 		WHERE [UserID] = @UserID
  		END
END
--Update 
ELSE IF @Action = 2 
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT [UserID] FROM Users WHERE [UserID] = @UserID)
		BEGIN
		UPDATE Users
		SET 
		[UserName] = @UserName,
		[Password] = @Password,
		[Email] = @Email,
		[LastPasswordChange] = @LastPasswordChange,
		[LastLoginDate] = @LastLoginDate,
		[DateCreate] = @DateCreate,
		[User_ToString] = @User_ToString,
		[Type] = @Type,
		[Active] = @Active
 		WHERE [UserID] = @UserID
  		END
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Users_ChangePassword] 
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
	@UserName nvarchar(50),
	@PasswordOld nvarchar(50),
	@PasswordNew nvarchar(50)
AS
BEGIN
	Update Users set Password=@PasswordNew Where UserName = @UserName and Password = @PasswordOld
END

CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Users_Search]
(
	@UserID int out, 
	@UserName nvarchar(50),	
	@Email nvarchar(100),	
	@Action int)
AS
--Search by Id
IF @Action = 0
	BEGIN
		SELECT * FROM Users WHERE UserID=@UserID
	END
--Search by UserName 
ELSE IF @Action = 1
BEGIN
	SELECT * FROM Users where UserName like '%'+@UserName+'%' 		  		
END
--Search by Email 
ELSE IF @Action = 2 
BEGIN
	SELECT * FROM Users where Email like '%'+@Email+'%'
END
GO

GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure Users_Paging    Generate Code Date: 6/17/2011 10:04:10 PM ******/CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Users_Paging]	@PageNumber  int,	@PageSize  intASDECLARE @_Users TABLE (	RowNumber INT IDENTITY (1,1), 	UserID               int, 	UserName             nvarchar(50), 	Password             nvarchar(50), 	Email                nvarchar(100), 	LastPasswordChange   datetime, 	LastLoginDate        datetime, 	DateCreate           datetime, 	User_ToString        nvarchar(100), 	Type                 nvarchar(50), 	Active               bit)INSERT INTO @_UsersSELECT UserID, UserName, Password, Email, LastPasswordChange, LastLoginDate, DateCreate, User_ToString, Type, ActiveFROM UsersSELECT COUNT (UserID) FROM @_UsersSELECT * FROM @_Users WHERE RowNumber > (@PageNumber -1) * @PageSize AND RowNumber <=@PageNumber * @PageSize
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Users_Login] 
@UserName nvarchar(1000),
@Password nvarchar(1000),
@Active bit
AS
BEGIN
Select * from [Users] where @UserName = UserName and @Password = Password and @Active=Active;
END

Create PROCEDURE [dbo].[Users_GetUserByGroupID] 
@GroupID int
AS
BEGIN
	select * from [Users] where UserID in (select UserID from InGroup where GroupID=@GroupID)
END
GO

create PROCEDURE [dbo].[Users_GetNotUserByGroupID] 
@GroupID int
AS
BEGIN
	select * from [Users] where UserID not in (select UserID from InGroup where GroupID=@GroupID)
END
GO

SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Users_CopyUser]
(
	@UserID int out, 
	@UserName nvarchar(50),	
	@Email nvarchar(100),
	@Total int,	
	@Action int)
AS
declare @count int
set @count=0
--Search by Id
IF @Action = 0
	BEGIN
		 
		IF EXISTS(SELECT UserID FROM Users WHERE UserID=@UserID)
		BEGIN			
			WHILE(@count < @Total)
			begin
				-- copy thong tin user				
				INSERT INTO Users(UserName,Password,Email,LastPasswordChange,LastLoginDate,DateCreate,User_ToString,Type,Active) 
				SELECT UserName,Password,Email,LastPasswordChange,LastLoginDate,DateCreate,User_ToString,Type,Active FROM Users WHERE UserID=@UserID
				Set @UserID = @@IDENTITY
				-- copy profile
				Insert INTO Profile(UserID) values(@UserID)				
				--set @ProfileID=@@IDENTITY
				set @count=@@IDENTITY
				print cast(@UserID as nvarchar(3))
			end
  		END
	END
--Search by UserName 
ELSE IF @Action = 1
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT * FROM Users WHERE UserName like '%'+@UserName+'%')
	BEGIN
		WHILE(@count < @Total)
			begin
				INSERT INTO Users(UserName,Password,Email,LastPasswordChange,LastLoginDate,DateCreate,User_ToString,Type,Active) 
				SELECT UserName,Password,Email,LastPasswordChange,LastLoginDate,DateCreate,User_ToString,Type,Active FROM Users WHERE UserName like '%'+@UserName+'%'
				Set @UserID = @@IDENTITY
				Insert INTO Profile(UserID) values(@UserID)				
				--set @ProfileID=@@IDENTITY
				set @count=@count+1
			end		
  	END
	--SELECT * FROM Users where UserName like '%'+@UserName+'%' 		  		
END
--Search by Email 
ELSE IF @Action = 2 
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT * FROM Users WHERE Email like '%'+@Email+'%')
	BEGIN
		WHILE(@count < @Total)
			begin
				INSERT INTO Users(UserName,Password,Email,LastPasswordChange,LastLoginDate,DateCreate,User_ToString,Type,Active) 
				SELECT UserName,Password,Email,LastPasswordChange,LastLoginDate,DateCreate,User_ToString,Type,Active FROM Users WHERE Email like '%'+@Email+'%'
				Set @UserID = @@IDENTITY
				Insert INTO Profile(UserID) values(@UserID)				
				--set @ProfileID=@@IDENTITY
				set @count=@count+1
			end
  	END
END
GO

(
	@ProfileID int out, 
	@UserID int,
	@FirstName nvarchar(100),
	@LastName nvarchar(50),	
	@Action int)
AS
--Search by ProfileID
IF @Action = 0
 BEGIN
	SELECT * FROM Profile where ProfileID=@ProfileID

ELSE IF @Action = 1

	SELECT * FROM Profile WHERE UserID = @UserID

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
------------------------------------------------------------------
------------------ Procedure Table Profile ---------------------------
------------------------------------------------------------------

 CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Profile_CreateDeleteUpdate]
(
	@ProfileID int out, 
	@UserID int,
	@FirstName nvarchar(100),
	@LastName nvarchar(50),
	@Department nvarchar(500),
	@Position nvarchar(500),
	@Image nvarchar(100),
	@Address nvarchar(500),
	@Phone nvarchar(15),
	@Birdthday datetime,
	@LastUpdateProfile datetime,
	@Country nvarchar(50),
	@Genre nvarchar(5),
	@Ethnic nvarchar(50),
	@Religion nvarchar(50),
	@Active bit,
	@Action int)
AS
--Create
IF @Action = 0
 BEGIN
 INSERT INTO Profile
	( [UserID], [FirstName], [LastName], [Department], [Position], [Image], [Address], [Phone], [Birdthday], [LastUpdateProfile], [Country], [Genre], [Ethnic], [Religion], [Active] )
 VALUES 
	( @UserID, @FirstName, @LastName, @Department, @Position, @Image, @Address, @Phone, @Birdthday, @LastUpdateProfile, @Country, @Genre, @Ethnic, @Religion, @Active)
 SET @ProfileID = @@IDENTITY
END
--Delete 
ELSE IF @Action = 1
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT [ProfileID] FROM Profile WHERE [ProfileID] = @ProfileID)
		BEGIN
		UPDATE Profile
		SET 		
		[Active] = 0
 		WHERE [ProfileID] = @ProfileID
  		END
END
--Update 
ELSE IF @Action = 2 
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT [ProfileID] FROM Profile WHERE [ProfileID] = @ProfileID)
		BEGIN
		UPDATE Profile
		SET 
		[UserID] = @UserID,
		[FirstName] = @FirstName,
		[LastName] = @LastName,
		[Department] = @Department,
		[Position] = @Position,
		[Image] = @Image,
		[Address] = @Address,
		[Phone] = @Phone,
		[Birdthday] = @Birdthday,
		[LastUpdateProfile] = @LastUpdateProfile,
		[Country] = @Country,
		[Genre] = @Genre,
		[Ethnic] = @Ethnic,
		[Religion] = @Religion,
		[Active] = @Active
 		WHERE [ProfileID] = @ProfileID
  		END
END
GO

 BEGIN
 INSERT INTO InRoles
	( [ApplicationID], [GroupID], [DateCreate], [Active] )

 SET @InRolesID = @@IDENTITY

 		WHERE [InRolesID] = @InRolesID

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure Log_Update    Generate Code Date: 6/17/2011 10:04:10 PM ******/CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Log_Update]	@LogID                int,	@UserID               int,	@Date                 datetime,	@Trace                nvarchar(200),	@IP                   nvarchar(50),	@Action               nvarchar(200),	@Time_Login           datetime,	@Time_Logout          datetimeASUPDATE Log SET 	UserID= @UserID,	Date= @Date,	Trace= @Trace,	IP= @IP,	Action= @Action,	Time_Login= @Time_Login,	Time_Logout= @Time_LogoutWHERE LogID = @LogID

GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure Log_Paging    Generate Code Date: 6/17/2011 10:04:10 PM ******/CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Log_Paging]	@PageNumber  int,	@PageSize  intASDECLARE @_Log TABLE (	RowNumber INT IDENTITY (1,1), 	LogID                int, 	UserID               int, 	Date                 datetime, 	Trace                nvarchar(200), 	IP                   nvarchar(50), 	Action               nvarchar(200), 	Time_Login           datetime, 	Time_Logout          datetime)INSERT INTO @_LogSELECT LogID, UserID, Date, Trace, IP, [Action], Time_Login, Time_Logout FROM Log order by LogID descSELECT COUNT (LogID) FROM @_LogSELECT * FROM @_Log WHERE RowNumber > (@PageNumber -1) * @PageSize AND RowNumber <=@PageNumber * @PageSize
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Log_CreateDeleteUpdate]
(
	@LogID int out, 
	@UserID int,
	@Date datetime,
	@Trace nvarchar(200),
	@IP nvarchar(50),
	@Action nvarchar(200),
	@Time_Login datetime,
	@Time_Logout datetime,
	@ActionQ int)
AS
--Create
IF @ActionQ = 0
 BEGIN
 INSERT INTO Log
	( [UserID], [Date], [Trace], [IP], [Action], [Time_Login], [Time_Logout] )
 VALUES 
	( @UserID, @Date, @Trace, @IP, @Action, @Time_Login, @Time_Logout)
 SET @LogID = @@IDENTITY
END
--Delete 
ELSE IF @ActionQ = 1
BEGIN
	DELETE Log WHERE [LogID] = @LogID
END
--Update 
ELSE IF @ActionQ = 2 
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT [LogID] FROM Log WHERE [LogID] = @LogID)
		BEGIN
		UPDATE Log
		SET 
		[UserID] = @UserID,
		[Date] = @Date,
		[Trace] = @Trace,
		[IP] = @IP,
		[Action] = @Action,
		[Time_Login] = @Time_Login,
		[Time_Logout] = @Time_Logout
 		WHERE [LogID] = @LogID
  		END
END
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON

 BEGIN
	 SELECT * FROM InGroup WHERE InGroupID=@InGroupID
END

	SELECT * FROM InGroup WHERE @GroupID=@GroupID
END
--Search by UserID 
ELSE IF @Action = 2 
BEGIN
	SELECT * FROM InGroup WHERE UserID=@UserID
END
GO

CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Application_GetByParentID]
(	
	@ParentID int
)
AS
	select * from InRoles inrol,(select * from Application Where @ParentID = Parent_Id and Active =1) p where inrol.ApplicationID = p.ApplicationID

 CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Group_GetByUserID]
(	
	@UserID int
)
AS
	select g.* from Groups g,(SELECT GroupID FROM InGroup WHERE UserID = @UserID) inGroup where g.GroupID=inGroup.GroupID and g.Active=1

 CREATE Procedure [dbo].[FilePermission_CreateDeleteUpdate]
(
	@FilePermissionID int out, 
	@PermissionID int,
	@GroupID int,
	@FolderPath nvarchar(200),
	@Action int)
AS
--Create
IF @Action = 0
 BEGIN
 INSERT INTO FilePermission
	( [PermissionID], [GroupID], [FolderPath] )
 VALUES 
	( @PermissionID, @GroupID, @FolderPath)
 SET @FilePermissionID = @@IDENTITY
END
--Delete 
ELSE IF @Action = 1
BEGIN
	DELETE FilePermission WHERE [FilePermissionID] = @FilePermissionID
END
--Update 
ELSE IF @Action = 2 
BEGIN
	IF EXISTS(SELECT [FilePermissionID] FROM FilePermission WHERE [FilePermissionID] = @FilePermissionID)
		BEGIN
		UPDATE FilePermission
		SET 
		[PermissionID] = @PermissionID,
		[GroupID] = @GroupID,
		[FolderPath] = @FolderPath
 		WHERE [FilePermissionID] = @FilePermissionID
  		END
END

CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Application_GetByUserID]
(	
	@UserID int
)
AS
	select ap.* from Application ap,(select inR.ApplicationID from InRoles inR,(SELECT GroupID FROM InGroup WHERE UserID = @UserID) inGroup where inGroup.GroupID = inR.GroupID and inR.Active=1) inrol where inrol.ApplicationID = ap.ApplicationID and ap.Active=1 Order by Parent_Id
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Application_GetByUser]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Application_GetByUser]
@UserID int
AS
BEGIN

Select * from [Application] where ApplicationID in(
select ApplicationID from InRoles where GroupID in (Select GroupID from InGroup where @UserID = UserID))

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Application_AllAppByGroups]    Script Date: 08/31/2011 15:02:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Application_AllAppByGroups]
	@GroupID int,
	@active bit
AS
BEGIN
	SELECT * from [Application] where ApplicationID in (select ApplicationID from InRoles where @GroupID = GroupID) and Active = @active
END
GO
